   in accordance with the regulations of the Convention on Biological
   Diversity and the Galapagos National Park. We are grateful to X.
   Aguirre, M. Bonifacio, N. Castillo, J. Crisci, F. JimEnez, J.
   Garcia-Franco, C. Maticorena, R. Oviedo, B. Peguero, E. Ruiz, P. Robayo,
   W. Simbana and E. Yanez for their help. Brett Jestrow and J. Moynihan
   assisted with the Bayesian analysis. Felix Forest, S. Stefanovic and V.
   Steinmann provided valuable information concerning the phylogenetics of
   Polygala, Cuscuta and Euphorbia, respectively. Bruce Baldwin and L.
   Collins (FIU) gave useful insights into the likelihood-ratio test and
   the palaeo-environments of Central America, respectively. Likewise, D.
   Geist provided information on the geology of the Galapagos Islands. This
   study was part of the MSc thesis of N.A., which was conducted under the
   supervision of J.F.-O. and sponsored by the graduate program on tropical
   botany jointly operated by FIU and FTBG. Michael Heads and an anonymous
   referee provided useful comments on the manuscript. This is contribution
   number 103 from TBP-FIU and contribution number 1077 from the Charles
   Darwin Research Station.
